# Sound Voltex Exceed Gear ã‚³ãƒŠã‚¹ãƒ† Charts

**Note: I am aware this webpage needs an update. I am in the process of rewriting the script which generates this list. As such, please be patient. ğŸ˜Š**

*SOUND VOLTEX EXCEED GEAR ã‚³ãƒŠã‚¹ãƒ†*, or EAC (*E-Amusement Cloud*) for short, comes with a large catalogue of charts, some of which come with the basic course *æœ€åˆã‹ã‚‰ãƒ—ãƒ¬ãƒ¼ã§ãã¾ã™*, and some of which come with purchasable packs [[1](https://p.eagate.573.jp/gate/p/eamusement/coop/list.html?shop=1&category=45&cc=1&ls=1), [2](https://p.eagate.573.jp/game/eacsdvx/vi/music/index.html)]. This page contains a table of all charts, as of {{ page.updated }}, as fetched from the main website [[2](https://p.eagate.573.jp/game/eacsdvx/vi/music/index.html)]. Ctrl+F can be used to search for a specific chart. This table allows for sorting; just click the header of a column to sort by that column (Made possible by the script from Stuart Langridge)[[3](https://www.kryogenix.org/code/browser/sorttable/)]. Charts can be inspected on [sdvx.in](https://sdvx.in/) by clicking the difficulty number of a chart. All charts have links, but some have not been mapped on the sdvx.in website however. In such a case an empty chart is shown. The *Released* column entries are added manually. Please notify me of mistakes.  

The *Pack* column specifies the chart packs as listed on the main website [[2](https://p.eagate.573.jp/game/eacsdvx/vi/music/index.html)]. Some charts are available for purchase through song packs, which can be purchased on the main *E-Amusement* portal [[1](https://p.eagate.573.jp/gate/p/eamusement/coop/list.html?shop=1&category=45&cc=1&ls=1)]. The *Released* column specifies when a chart was released, and under which unlock conditions, or extras. If a chart does not have a date specified, it is not available to new players. However, users who played the *GRAVITY WARS ã‚³ãƒŠã‚¹ãƒ†* version of the game may have these charts unlocked [*Citation needed*].

{% include article_block.html %}

<br>

### Glossary

|Term|Meaning|
|:-|:-|
|AC Unlock|By playing these charts in the specified time period, they can be unlocked for play on the arcade version of the game. Check the main website for more details [[4](https://p.eagate.573.jp/game/eacsdvx/vi/news/index.html)]. Listed under *Released*.|
|Basic Course|These charts are available with the monthly subscription. Listed under *Pack*.|
|BLASTER GATE|Collect *BLASTER ENERGY* to gain access to the *BLASTER GATE* unlock procedure. Charts may be unlocked after a single play during events, regardless of the passing grade was obtained. Stay up to date with events on the main website [[4](https://p.eagate.573.jp/game/eacsdvx/vi/news/index.html)]. Listed under *Released*.|
|BLASTER Release|Charts which were newly released as *BLASTER GATE* unlockables in the specified month. Listed under *Pack*.|
|Member Unlock|Charts in these packs were released to monthly subscribers of the *GRAVITY WARS* version of konaste in the specified month. Some of these charts are re-released to *EXCEED GEAR* through the *BLASTER GATE*. Listed under *Pack*.|

<br>
